        <script>
            jQuery(function($) {
                //redirectOldBrowserToUpgrade();
            });
            
            function redirectOldBrowserToUpgrade() {
                if ($.browser.msie && $.browser.version<11) {
                    window.location.replace("/manager/login/upgrade_browser.php");
                }
                if ($.browser.mozilla && $.browser.version<38) {
                    window.location.replace("/manager/login/upgrade_browser.php");
                }
                if (jQBrowser.uaMatch().name=='safari' && $.browser.versionNumber<8) {
                    window.location.replace("/manager/login/upgrade_browser.php");
                }
                if (jQBrowser.uaMatch().name=='chrome' && $.browser.versionNumber<40) {
                    window.location.replace("/manager/login/upgrade_browser.php");
                }
            }
        </script>
        <script>
            jQuery(function($) {
                //Send help window form
                $("#helpWindowAjax").submit(function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault(); // avoid to execute the actual submit of the form.
            
                    $.ajax({
                      type: "POST",
                      url: "/manager/supportO.php",
                      data: $('#helpWindowAjax').serialize(),
                      success: function(data) {
                        //Show success message
                        $.gritter.add({
                          title: 'The message sent to us. BIG SMILE TO YOU :)',
                          class_name: 'gritter-success',
                          time: 6000
                        });
            
                        //Close window
                        $('#helpWindow').modal('hide');
                      }
                    });
                });
                
                $('#tellWorld').on('show.bs.modal', function (event) {
            
                    var modal = $(this);
                    
                    //We don't reload the window every time it open, only for the first time.
                    if (modal.find('.modal-body .col-md-12').html()=='') {
                        modal.find('.modal-body .col-md-12').html('<iframe id="shareWindow" src="/manager/shareUs.php" style="width:100%;height:450px;margin:0;padding:0;border:none;"></iframe>');
                    }
            
                    mixPanelEvent(false,"Click tell your friend button");
                });
            
                //Agency account
                $('.agency_Buttons').on('click', function(event) {//Prevent the anchor action
                    event.preventDefault();
            
                    var $this = $(this);
            
                    if ($this.attr('disabled')=='disabled') {
                        return;
                    }
            
                    var href = $this.attr('href');
                    var title = $this.data('agency-title');
            
                    // Cross Domain - On dashboard we got cross domain so we handle it here
                    var crossDomain = top.location.href.toLowerCase().indexOf('/dashboard.php') !== -1;
                    if ( href.indexOf('?') === -1 ) {
                      href += '?crossDomain=' + crossDomain;
                    } else {
                      href += '&crossDomain=' + crossDomain;
                    }
                    
                    $('#agencyAccount').find('.modal-body').html('<iframe id="agencyAccountList" src="'+href+'" style="width:100%;height:500px;margin:0;padding:0;border:none;"></iframe>');
                    $('#agencyAccount').find('.modal-title').html(title);
                    $('#agencyAccount').modal('show');
                });
            });
            
            //Close the pop-up and redirect to the new team
            function CloseAgencyPopupAndRedirect(agencyID) {
                $('#agencyAccount').modal('hide');
                location.href = '/manager/sites.php';
            }
            
            //Close the pop-up and reload the agency page
            function CloseAgencyPopupAndReload(agencyID) {
                $('#agencyAccount').modal('hide');
                location.reload();
            }
        </script>

                (function(){var w=window;var ic=w.Intercom;if(typeof ic==="function"){ic('reattach_activator');ic('update',intercomSettings);}else{var d=document;var i=function(){i.c(arguments)};i.q=[];i.c=function(args){i.q.push(args)};w.Intercom=i;function l(){var s=d.createElement('script');s.type='text/javascript';s.async=true;s.src='https://widget.intercom.io/widget/jokji8l9';var x=d.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];x.parentNode.insertBefore(s,x);}if(w.attachEvent){w.attachEvent('onload',l);}else{w.addEventListener('load',l,false);}}})()

            //Hide intercom before we show it so we can manage it
            Intercom('hide');
            
            Intercom('onUnreadCountChange', function(unreadCount) {
                //Add a class to the button so when the user will click on it we will open the Intercom window
                if (unreadCount>0) {
                    $('.help247window').addClass('forceIntercom');
                }
            });
            
            //We make sure that when Intercom show we add CLOSE button to the interface
            Intercom('onShow', function() {   
                $('.help247window').hide(function() {
                    $('.help247close').show(100); 
                });
                //FIX RTL problem
                FixIntercomRTL();
                //Hide our help center popup
                $('.helpBOX-popup').hide(100);
                //Remove the force class if the user open it from a message
                $('.help247window').removeClass('forceIntercom');
            });
            
            Intercom('onHide', function() {   
                CloseAllHelpCenterWindows();
            });
        </script>

        <script>
            jQuery(function($) {
                $('.help247window').click(function() {
                    //If Intercom send us message we first show Intercom window and not our message
                    if ($('.forceIntercom').length>0) {
                        Intercom('showMessages');
                    } else {
                        //We show our support window
                        $('.helpBOX-popup').show(100);
                    }  
                    $('.help247window').hide(function() {
                        $('.help247close').show(100); 
                    });  
                });
                $('.help247close').click(function() {
                    Intercom('hide');
                    CloseAllHelpCenterWindows();
                });
                $('.intercomButton').click(function() {
                    Intercom('show');
                });
            });
            
            function FixIntercomRTL() {
                if ($('html[dir=rtl]').length>0) {
                    setTimeout(function() {
                        $('.intercom-messenger-frame').attr('style','left: 20px !important;right: auto !important;');
                    },50);
                    setTimeout(function() {
                        $('.intercom-messenger-frame').attr('style','left: 20px !important;right: auto !important;');
                    },300);
                }
            }
            
            function CloseAllHelpCenterWindows() {
                //Remove the class that force this window
                $('.help247window').removeClass('forceIntercom');
                $('.helpBOX-popup').hide(100);
                $('.help247close').hide(function() {
                    $('.help247window').show(100); 
                });
            }
        </script>

<script>
	var speechWorking = false;
	jQuery(function($) {
		window.SpeechRecognition = window.SpeechRecognition        ||
								window.webkitSpeechRecognition  ||
								null;
		if (!SpeechRecognition) {
			document.querySelector('.js-api-support').removeAttribute('hidden');
			document.querySelector('.js-api-info').setAttribute('hidden', '');
			[].forEach.call(document.querySelectorAll('form button'), function(button) {
				button.setAttribute('disabled', '');
			});
		} else {
			var recognizer = new SpeechRecognition();
			var transcription = document.getElementById('transcription');
			// Start recognising
			recognizer.addEventListener('result', function(event) {
				transcription.textContent = '';
				for (var i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {
					//if (event.results[i].isFinal) {
						//transcription.textContent = event.results[i][0].transcript + ' (Confidence: ' + event.results[i][0].confidence + ')';
					//} else {
						transcription.textContent += event.results[i][0].transcript;
					//}
				}
				transcription.textContent = transcription.textContent.trim().toLowerCase();

				$('[data-speech="on"]').each(function() {
					$this   = $(this);
					$id     = $this.attr('id');
					$text   = $this.data('speech-text').trim().toLowerCase();

					if (transcription.textContent==$text) {
						$this.trigger( 'click' );
					}
				});
				console.log('This what I heard: '+transcription.textContent);
			});
			// Listen for errors
			recognizer.addEventListener('error', function(event) {
				console.log('Recognition error: ' + event.message);
			});
			recognizer.addEventListener('end', function() {
				console.log('Recognition ended');
			});
			document.getElementById('button-play').addEventListener('click', function() {
				if (speechWorking==true) {
					speechWorking = false;
					$('#words_you_can_speak').hide();
					try {
						recognizer.stop();
						console.log('Recognition stopped');
						$('#button-play').html('<i class="fa fa-microphone"></i>');
					} catch(ex) {
						console.log('Recognition error: ' + ex.message);
					}
				} else {
					speechWorking = true;
					$('#words_you_can_speak').show();
					transcription.textContent = '';
					// Set if we need interim results
					var isInterimResults = document.querySelector('input[name="recognition-type"][value="interim"]').checked;
					recognizer.lang = $('#languageSpeech').val();
					recognizer.continuous = !isInterimResults;
					recognizer.interimResults = isInterimResults;
					try {
						recognizer.start();
						console.log('Recognition started');
						$('#button-play').html('<i class="fa fa-microphone-slash"></i>');
					} catch(ex) {
						console.log('Recognition error: ' + ex.message);
					}
				}
			});
		}
	});
</script>
